# ChaseOS CLI Operator Handbook

> Generated by `python -m runtime.cli.generate_docs --write`.
> Do not hand-edit command coverage. Update the command contract, ratchet specs, or operator handbook metadata.

**Approval Center routing:** generated approval-center and approval-queue command references should point operators to [[ChaseOS-Approval-Center]] for current cross-feature Approval Center semantics.

This handbook is the operator-facing companion to `ChaseOS-CLI-Command-Reference.md`. It explains what each command is for, how it is expected to be used, and how the CLI ratchet currently treats it.

## Ratchet Status Legend

- `ratchet-smoked`: representative command is executed by `chaseos test cli-contract`.
- `family-deferred`: the command family has known safety, fixture, readiness, or normalization blockers recorded in the deferred closure map.
- `closed_...` deferred entries are intentionally not routine-smoked and have a representative safe smoke plus a promotion boundary.
- `contract/docs only`: parser, contract, action, and docs are checked, but no live smoke is run.
- `covered by family ratchet`: another command in the same family represents this command's parser/JSON surface.

## Deferred Smoke Closure Map

These entries are intentionally excluded from routine smoke execution. Each one must keep a representative smoke, fixture/readiness posture, forbidden ratchet actions, and promotion condition so deferrals stay auditable.

| Deferred command | Status | Blocker | Representative smoke | Fixture readiness | Forbidden during ratchet | Promotion condition |
|------------------|--------|---------|----------------------|-------------------|--------------------------|---------------------|
| `chaseos n8n execute` | `closed_by_n8n_readiness_and_dry_run_smokes` | `execution_adjacent` | `n8n.dry-run` | n8n readiness validates config/registry without HTTP; n8n dry-run validates a call draft without live execution or writes | workflow_execution, live_http_call, connector_call, external_side_effect | do not promote live execute into routine smoke; live execution requires explicit operator approval and a separate governed runner proof |
| `chaseos capture ...` | `closed_by_capture_status_and_validate_smokes` | `mutating_or_external` | `capture.validate` | packaged intake fixture vault covers capture status and validate-only posture without quarantine writes, connector calls, or external fetches | quarantine_write, connector_call, external_fetch, dedup_registry_write | do not promote mutating/external capture commands into routine smoke; add separate no-write validate surfaces for any future capture mode |

## acquisition

Build and inspect governed acquisition and normalization inputs before they become workflow-ready operating packets.

**Ratchet disposition:** `smoke_covered`

**Real-world use case:** Use acquisition commands when checking whether research or source material is ready for a briefing, digest, or downstream workflow.

## audit

Run repo-safe audits that classify risky references without exposing raw secrets or mutating vault state.

**Ratchet disposition:** `contract_docs_only`

**Real-world use case:** Use audit commands when validating secret hygiene boundaries with placeholders, sentinels, and private-env skips before trusting a release or runtime handoff.

| Command | Purpose | Example | Safety | Ratchet | Real-world scenario |
|---------|---------|---------|--------|---------|---------------------|
| `chaseos audit secrets [--vault-root PATH] [--max-files N] [--json]` | Classify placeholder/sentinel secret references separately from high-confidence live secrets while skipping private env files and aliases. | `python -m runtime.cli.main audit secrets --vault-root runtime/cli/fixtures/secret_audit_vault --json` | `mutating-or-execution-adjacent` | `contract/docs only` | Use this as a bounded read-only secret hygiene check; results redact matches and report private-env skips rather than reading or emitting raw env values. |

| `chaseos mvp operator-action-required [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Show whether operator-owned input is currently blocking MVP completion, including the canonical no-secret handoff card path. | `python -m runtime.cli.main mvp operator-action-required --json` | `read-only` | `contract/docs only` | Use this as the stop/continue gate when Codex may be out of safe autonomous MVP passes. |

| `chaseos mvp validate-operator-input --input PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Validate a filled no-secret MVP operator input packet without echoing candidate values or executing follow-up actions. | `python -m runtime.cli.main mvp validate-operator-input --input operator-input.json --json` | `read-only` | `contract/docs only` | Use this after filling the operator input template to check references, paths, and decisions before any setup write, VentureOps authoring, or approval consumption. |

## run

Launch or dry-run governed AOR workflows through ChaseOS workflow manifests.

**Ratchet disposition:** `smoke_covered`

**Real-world use case:** Use run commands when invoking operator workflows such as daily briefs, closeout, graph hygiene, or idea graduation.

| Command | Purpose | Example | Safety | Ratchet | Real-world scenario |
|---------|---------|---------|--------|---------|---------------------|
| `chaseos run WORKFLOW_ID [--date YYYY-MM-DD] [--output-format markdown|json] [--input KEY=VALUE] [--adapter ADAPTER_ID] [--coordination-via runtime/agent_bus/] [--dry-run] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Run. | `chaseos run WORKFLOW_ID [--date YYYY-MM-DD] [--output-format markdown|json] [--input KEY=VALUE] [--adapter ADAPTER_ID] [--coordination-via runtime/agent_bus/] [--dry-run] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `mutating-or-execution-adjacent` | `ratchet-smoked: run.operator_today.dry-run` | Use run commands when invoking operator workflows such as daily briefs, closeout, graph hygiene, or idea graduation. |

## runtime

Inspect runtime status, lifecycle health, provider governance, startup surfaces, and runtime coordination.

**Ratchet disposition:** `smoke_covered`

**Real-world use case:** Use runtime commands when diagnosing the local operating layer before dispatching work.

| Command | Purpose | Example | Safety | Ratchet | Real-world scenario |

## studio

Inspect or operate ChaseOS Studio product surfaces, QA runners, approval previews, and read-only panel contracts.

**Ratchet disposition:** `smoke_covered`

**Real-world use case:** Use studio commands when validating the native Studio shell, panel contracts, or approval-gated product workflows.

## subagents

Inspect task-scoped sub-agent presets, preview ChaseOS runtime routing, build review-only approval packet previews, and optionally write pending approval requests without dispatch.

**Ratchet disposition:** `smoke_covered`

**Real-world use case:** Use sub-agent commands when choosing a bounded preset, validating runtime availability, previewing which ChaseOS runtime would receive a task, or preparing a governed pending approval request for operator review.

| Command | Purpose | Example | Safety | Ratchet | Real-world scenario |
|---------|---------|---------|--------|---------|---------------------|
| `chaseos subagents agent-bus-task-packet-preview --approval-artifact-path PATH --decision-artifact-path PATH [--consumption-marker-path PATH] [--expected-work-fingerprint SHA256] [--sender NAME] [--priority low|normal|high|critical] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Preview the inert Agent Bus task packet that would be enqueued after request, decision, and marker artifacts are bound. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents agent-bus-task-packet-preview --approval-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/example.json --decision-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/_decisions/example.json --consumption-marker-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/_consumption_markers/example.json --expected-work-fingerprint SHA256 --json` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this after an exact-once marker is recorded to inspect the future Agent Bus packet shape. The command never creates a bus task, starts a daemon, dispatches a runtime, calls providers, or mutates canonical state. |
| `chaseos subagents approval-consumption-decision-binding --approval-artifact-path PATH --decision-artifact-path PATH [--expected-work-fingerprint SHA256] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Validate a pending sub-agent approval request plus a recorded approved decision artifact without consuming either artifact. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents approval-consumption-decision-binding --approval-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/example.json --decision-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/_decisions/example.json --expected-work-fingerprint SHA256 --json` | `approval-governed` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this after approval-review-decision writes an approved decision artifact to prove the decision-bound consumption preflight is ready for a future executor while approval consumption, marker writing, Agent Bus enqueue, daemon start, runtime dispatch, provider calls, and canonical writes remain blocked. |
| `chaseos subagents approval-consumption-dry-run --approval-artifact-path PATH [--expected-work-fingerprint SHA256] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Validate a pending sub-agent approval request artifact, exact work fingerprint, recomputed route, and future marker path without consuming approval. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents approval-consumption-dry-run --approval-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/example.json --expected-work-fingerprint SHA256 --json` | `approval-governed` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this after a pending approval request artifact exists to prove the future consumption boundary and show that operator approval decision, Agent Bus enqueue, daemon start, runtime dispatch, provider calls, and canonical writes remain blocked. |
| `chaseos subagents approval-consumption-exact-once-marker-contract --approval-artifact-path PATH --decision-artifact-path PATH [--expected-work-fingerprint SHA256] [--write-consumption-marker] [--consumed-by ID] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Preview or write one exact-once approval consumption marker after a pending request and approved decision artifact are bound. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents approval-consumption-exact-once-marker-contract --approval-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/example.json --decision-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/_decisions/example.json --expected-work-fingerprint SHA256 --write-consumption-marker --json` | `approval-governed` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this after approval-consumption-decision-binding is ready to reserve the exact-once marker for a future executor. The command does not mutate the request or decision artifacts and still blocks Agent Bus enqueue, daemon start, runtime dispatch, provider calls, and canonical writes. |
| `chaseos subagents approval-preview PRESET_ID [--mode MODE] [--task-id TASK_ID] [--objective TEXT] [--requested-by ID] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Build a deterministic, review-only approval packet preview for future sub-agent activation or Agent Bus enqueue. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents approval-preview site-ops-worker --mode site_ops --json` | `approval-governed` | `ratchet-smoked: subagents.approval-preview` | Use this when an operator needs the exact preset, mode, route, blocked effects, and work fingerprint before any approval artifact writer or executor exists. |
| `chaseos subagents approval-review-decision --approval-artifact-path PATH --decision approve|approved|deny|denied [--reviewer-id ID] [--reason TEXT] [--expected-work-fingerprint SHA256] [--write-approval-decision] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Preview or write one immutable approve/deny decision artifact for a pending sub-agent activation approval request without consuming approval. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents approval-review-decision --approval-artifact-path 07_LOGS/Agent-Activity/_subagent_activation_approvals/example.json --decision approve --expected-work-fingerprint SHA256 --write-approval-decision --json` | `approval-governed` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this after approval-consumption-dry-run validates the pending request and the operator wants to record a decision artifact only. The command still blocks approval consumption, Agent Bus enqueue, daemon start, runtime dispatch, provider calls, and canonical writes. |
| `chaseos subagents list [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | List task-scoped ChaseOS sub-agent presets and safe authority flags. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents list --json` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this before selecting a preset for a bounded task or team template. |
| `chaseos subagents route-preview PRESET_ID [--mode MODE] [--task-id TASK_ID] [--objective TEXT] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Preview the selected runtime and activation context for one preset without dispatch. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents route-preview site-ops-worker --mode site_ops --json` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this when deciding whether a task should route to Hermes, OpenClaw, Codex, or Archon before creating any bus task. |
| `chaseos subagents show PRESET_ID [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Show one sub-agent preset contract without starting a runtime. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents show qa-testing-worker --json` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use this when reviewing the allowed modes, runtime preferences, and writeback policy for one preset. |
| `chaseos subagents validate [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Validate sub-agent preset structure and runtime availability without execution or writes. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents validate --json` | `read-only` | `ratchet-smoked: subagents.validate` | Use this after editing preset files or runtime capability declarations. |
| `chaseos subagents write-approval-request PRESET_ID [--mode MODE] [--task-id TASK_ID] [--objective TEXT] [--requested-by ID] [--expected-work-fingerprint SHA256] [--write-approval-request] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Build or write a pending sub-agent activation approval request only when the exact approval-preview work fingerprint is supplied. | `python -m runtime.cli.main subagents write-approval-request site-ops-worker --mode site_ops --expected-work-fingerprint SHA256 --write-approval-request --json` | `approval-governed` | `ratchet-smoked: subagents.write-approval-request` | Use this after reviewing approval-preview output to persist a governed pending approval artifact without granting approval, consuming approval, creating an Agent Bus task, starting a daemon, dispatching a runtime, or calling a provider. |

## test

Run ChaseOS-local verification targets such as the CLI contract ratchet.

**Ratchet disposition:** `contract_docs_only`

**Real-world use case:** Use test commands when proving that parser, contract, docs, JSON actions, and representative smokes are aligned.

| Command | Purpose | Example | Safety | Ratchet | Real-world scenario |
|---------|---------|---------|--------|---------|---------------------|
| `chaseos test capture` | Test capture. | `chaseos test capture` | `read-only` | `contract/docs only` | Use test commands when proving that parser, contract, docs, JSON actions, and representative smokes are aligned. |
| `chaseos test cli-contract [--no-smoke] [--json]` | Run the direct CLI contract ratchet. | `python -m runtime.cli.main test cli-contract --json` | `mutating-or-execution-adjacent` | `contract/docs only` | Use this in development when parser, command contract, generated docs, JSON actions, or smoke profiles may have drifted. |

## watch

Inspect and operate watched-folder intake automation.

**Ratchet disposition:** `smoke_covered`

**Real-world use case:** Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline.

| Command | Purpose | Example | Safety | Ratchet | Real-world scenario |
|---------|---------|---------|--------|---------|---------------------|
| `chaseos watch add PATH --class clipboard|digest|journal|notebooklm|source|transcript|youtube_note [--source SOURCE] [--ext EXT] [--workspace WORKSPACE] [--domain DOMAIN] [--project PROJECT] [--topic TOPIC] [--origin-kind KIND] [--output-kind KIND] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Watch add. | `chaseos watch add PATH --class clipboard|digest|journal|notebooklm|source|transcript|youtube_note [--source SOURCE] [--ext EXT] [--workspace WORKSPACE] [--domain DOMAIN] [--project PROJECT] [--topic TOPIC] [--origin-kind KIND] [--output-kind KIND] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline. |
| `chaseos watch disable PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Watch disable. | `chaseos watch disable PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline. |
| `chaseos watch enable PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Watch enable. | `chaseos watch enable PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline. |
| `chaseos watch list [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Watch list. | `chaseos watch list [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `read-only` | `ratchet-smoked: watch.list` | Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline. |
| `chaseos watch remove PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Watch remove. | `chaseos watch remove PATH [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline. |
| `chaseos watch run [--once] [--interval N] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | Watch run. | `chaseos watch run [--once] [--interval N] [--vault-root PATH] [--json]` | `read-only` | `covered by family ratchet` | Use watch commands when managing local folder watches that feed the quarantine-first capture pipeline. |
